|1643|markcor|Adding noautoupdate reg entry   This is 2 fold to prevent updates on WIn 10 nodes. pauseupdate will pause updates, and Donnotupdate will prevent the updates from being downloaded with out human interaction if the pause is turned off. This tricky because the Windows Automatic Update service needs to run for OCC, so at the time of the run the machine is vulnerable to updates.  Updates cause 2 immediate problems; They cause an increase in disk space and can knock the Intel card out of use.|[URL](https://github.com/mozilla-releng/OpenCloudConfig/commit/ace8ea3884d82ac35f4f73d5abe0669cc9c39162)|2018-03-30 18:24:53

[taskcluster 2017-12-04T18:53:35.685Z]       "go-arch": "amd64", [taskcluster 2017-12-04T18:53:35.685Z]       "go-os": "windows", [taskcluster 2017-12-04T18:53:35.685Z]       "go-version": "go1.7.5", [taskcluster 2017-12-04T18:53:35.685Z]       "release": "https://github.com/taskcluster/generic-worker/releases/tag/v10.0.5", [taskcluster 2017-12-04T18:53:35.685Z]       "version": "10.0.5" [taskcluster 2017-12-04T18:53:35.685Z]     } [taskcluster 2017-12-04T18:53:35.685Z]   } [taskcluster 2017-12-04T18:53:35.685Z] Task ID: TVjKVAvaSk-q_1BiWr730g  The generic-worker version shows as 10.0.5 even though the manifest for this worker type installs generic-worker 10.2.3. It turned out that us-west-1 wasn't configured as a copy region in OpenCloudConfig for gecko-t-win10-64-gpu-b and thus it did not get updated when this worker type was deployed. The AMI it was using in us-west-1 was six months old.
